A tax crime investigation is conducted based on evidence and indicators of suspicion obtained from all sources, which determine that an enterprise has committed a tax offense. This is done within the statute of limitations for investigating misdemeanor, which is five years. Tax offenses are classified as misdemeanor. If there is evidence and indicators of suspicion confirming that the enterprise committed the offense, the General Department of Taxation will prepare and initiate an investigation file in accordance with legal procedures at any time.

Reference:

-┬а┬а ┬аSection 2.1, Chapter 2 of Manual on Tax Crime Investigation for Tax Officials and Taxpayers dated 9 April, 2024.

#### рЪАрЪа. What does the company misconduct which lead to tax investigation?

The offenses that lead to a tax crime investigation are as follows:

1.┬а┬а ┬аРђюTax EvasionРђЮ refers to any acts committed with willful and premeditated organized with the intention of eliminating the tax amount that required to pay.

There shall be also deem as negligence on any case as follows:

-┬а┬а ┬аThe serious negligence as stated in Article 224 of LOT which is committed two separate occasions within a period of 3 (three) calendar years.

-┬а┬а ┬аThe serious negligence as stated in Article 224 of LOT which is committed three or more separate occasions within a period of 10 (ten) calendar years.

2.┬а┬а ┬аSome of the РђюObstructing the Implementation of the Tax ProvisionРђЮ including:

-┬а┬а ┬аAttempts to obstruct the assessment or the tax collection.

-┬а┬а ┬аMaking or providing fraudulent records, documents, reports, or other information.

-┬а┬а ┬аConceals or deliberately destroys book of accounts, records, documents, reports or other information.

-┬а┬а ┬аIssue the fraudulent invoices.

-┬а┬а ┬аFailure to allow the tax administration to enter the business to determine and collect taxes.

3.┬а┬а ┬аSome activities are as following:

-┬а┬а ┬аProfessional as Tax Agent without License

-┬а┬а ┬аFailure to pay the collected tax

-┬а┬а ┬аTax collection without permission.

References:

-┬а┬а ┬аArticle 224, 225, 226, 245, 246, 247, 249 and Article 250 of the Law on Taxation, promulgated by Royal Decree No. NS/RKM0523/004 dated May 16, 2023.

#### ръЪрЪєръјръйръџ ръЊръиръёръЁръўрЪњръЏръЙръЎ ръЪрЪњръЈръИръќръИръђръХръџръЈръХръўръіръХръЊръЊръиръёръђръХръџръіръХръђрЪІръ»ръђръЪръХръџръЪрЪњръЊръЙръЪръ╗рЪєръЊръХръЊръХ

#### рЪА. How can enterprises or individuals submit application letters to the General Department of Taxation?

Enterprises or individuals who wish to submit an application letter to the General Department of Taxation may do so via the following methods:

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аDirect submission of the application letter to the General Department of Taxation.

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аSubmission through the GDT e-Administration electronic platform.

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аSubmission through the CamDX information technology platform (For enterprises requesting permanent business closure).

Reference:

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аInstruction No. 11936 GDT, dated March 21, 2024 РђЊ On the use of the GDT e-Administration platform.

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аInstruction No. 32775 GDT, dated September 17, 2024 РђЊ On the procedure for requesting permanent business closure.

#### рЪб. After submitting an application letter, how can enterprises or individuals track the progress of their application?

Progress of submitted applications can be tracked through the following channels:

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аUsing the GDT Check and Track App by scanning the QR Code received upon submission of the application to the General Department of Taxation.

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аContacting the GDT Call Center at 1277.

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аUsing GDT Live Chat.

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аVisiting the General Department of Taxation in person, bringing the submitted application letter stamped by the GDT.

Reference:

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аInstruction No. 27891 GDT, dated December 13, 2019 РђЊ Regarding the launch of the Document Checking & Tracking App for documents submitted to GDT.

#### рЪБ. What documents are required for notification of power of Attorney?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate, VAT registration certificate, and tax agent license (if authorized is a legal entity)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аNational ID card or passport (if ┬аauthorized is an individual)

Reference: None

#### рЪц. What documents are required to request a tax audit?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аMonthly and annual tax declaration (relevant to the audit period)

Reference: None

#### рЪЦ. What documents are required to request VAT refund?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аVAT refund application printed from the E-Filing system (original with company stamp and signature)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аAdditional documents as required in the VAT refund application form

Reference:

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аPrakas No. 576 MEF dated June 19, 2018 РђЊ On VAT refund mechanisms

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аInstruction No. 018 MEF.GDT dated August 8, 2023 РђЊ On procedures for tax credit and VAT refund applications

#### рЪд. What documents are required to request amendment of tax declaration?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аMonthly or annual tax declarations before and after amendment (with company signature and stamp)

Reference: None

#### рЪД. What documents are required to apply for a Tax Agent License?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication form for Tax Agent License (downloadable from www.tax.gov.kh)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аNational ID card, passport, or birth certificate

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аCertificate of commercial registration from Ministry of Commerce

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аArticles of incorporation of the company

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аCertificate of passing the Tax Agent examination or

License for accounting and auditing services issued by the Ministry of Economy and Finance or

Certificate of membership from the Kampuchea Institute of Certified Public Accountants and Auditors (KICPAA) or

Certificate of 10+ years of experience from the General Department of Taxation

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аDocument proving the location of the tax service operation (lease agreement or property ownership title)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аCurrent Tax Agent License (if applying for renewal)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аList of employees and clients receiving tax services and communication channels

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аTax payment receipts (white receipts)

Reference:

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аPrakas No. 230 MEF dated April 27, 2022 РђЊ On Tax Agent Services

#### рЪе. What documents are required for a tax exemption or tax reduction under the DTA agreement?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication form for exemption or reduction under DTA

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аCertificate of Incorporation (of the original company)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аCertificate of Residence (endorsed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs or embassy)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аContract/documents related to income payment

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аAuthorization letter

Reference: None

#### рЪЕ. What documents are required to apply for Income Tax Holiday?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аNational ID card or passport of the enterprise owner (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPermanent Registration Certificate from the Council for the Development of Cambodia or relevant institution

Reference:

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аPrakas No. 578 MEF.GDT dated September 19, 2024 РђЊ On Income Tax

#### рЪАрЪа. What documents are required to request 0% VAT on supplies to the garment, textile, footwear, bag, and hat industries?

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication letter

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT registration certificate (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аNational ID card or passport of the enterprise owner (if available)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аApplication form for 0% VAT implementation for goods/services for export purposes

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPermanent Registration Certificate from the CDC or relevant institution

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPrevious 0% VAT approval letter from GDT (not required for new applicants)

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аExport guarantee letter or supply contract from the subcontracting company

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPatent certificate and VAT certificate of the subcontractor

Рђб┬а┬а ┬аPermanent Registration Certificate of the subcontractor from CDC or relevant institution

Reference:

№ђГ┬а┬а ┬аPrakas No. 311 MEF dated March 19, 2014 РђЊ On VAT implementation for supporting industries or sub-contractors supplying goods/services to export-oriented garment, textile, footwear, bag, and hat industries
